\uff01 // \u201cTaiwanese Opera\u201d (ge zai xi) performed in front of a temple is one of the disappearing traditional custom in Taiwan. Swinging a fan at summer night and sitting on a stool to enjoy the opera, listening to grotesque stories from actors. In the time without films and TVs, it was the best entertainment in people\u2019s life.\n\nTaiwanese Opera (ge zai xi), which is the only one traditional drama stems from Taiwan, performing with Taiwanese Hokkien. Its music, action of actors, story and dressing are full of local Taiwanese features. Grace will guide you to understand this Taiwanese traditional culture from the front and back stage of the drama.\n\nPublic Beta for FREE is available for signing up NOW!\nMeeting Time and Place: 4 \\uff01 // \\u201cTaiwanese Opera\\u201d (ge zai xi) performed in front of a temple is one of the disappearing traditional custom in Taiwan. Swinging a fan at summer night and sitting on a stool to enjoy the opera, listening to grotesque stories from actors. In the time without films and TVs, it was the best entertainment in people\\u2019s life. Taiwanese Opera (ge zai xi), which is the only one traditional drama stems from Taiwan, performing with Taiwanese Hokkien. Its music, action of actors, story and dressing are full of local Taiwanese features. Grace will guide you to understand this Taiwanese traditional culture from the front and back stage of the drama. Public Beta for FREE is available for signing up NOW!
